[1m[38;5;1mfunction slugify(text) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return text[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        .toString()                          // Convert to string[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        .toLowerCase()                       // Convert to lowercase[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        .trim()                              // Trim leading and trailing whitespace[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        .replace(/\s+/g, '-')                // Replace spaces with -[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        .replace(/[^\w\-]+/g, '')            // Remove all non-word chars[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        .replace(/\-\-+/g, '-');             // Replace multiple - with single -[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1mfunction getComplementaryColor(hexColor) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Remove the hash at the start if it's there[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    hexColor = hexColor.replace(/^#/, '');[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Parse the r, g, b values[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let r = parseInt(hexColor.substr(0, 2), 16);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let g = parseInt(hexColor.substr(2, 2), 16);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let b = parseInt(hexColor.substr(4, 2), 16);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Calculate the brightness (perceived luminance)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Using the formula: 0.299*R + 0.587*G + 0.114*B[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let brightness = 0.299 * r + 0.587 * g + 0.114 * b;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Determine the complementary color based on brightness[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let complementaryColor;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (brightness < 128) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // If the color is dark, return white[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        complementaryColor = '#FFFFFF';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // If the color is bright, return black[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        complementaryColor = '#000000';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return complementaryColor;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m// Function to convert HEX to RGBA[0m
[1m[38;5;1mfunction hexToRgba(hex, alpha) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Remove the leading '#' if present[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    hex = hex.replace('#', '');[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Parse the red, green, blue values[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let r = parseInt(hex.substring(0, 2), 16);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let g = parseInt(hex.substring(2, 4), 16);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let b = parseInt(hex.substring(4, 6), 16);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1mfunction getRandomColor() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let color = '#';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return color;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1mfunction delay(time) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, time));[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1masync function handleRetrieveConcepts() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    await delay(500);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const concepts = await store.getResourceAsync(myAgent.subject);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const classes = concepts.get("https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/property/knows-concepts");[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let buttonGroups = {};[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let buttonHTML = '<div class="bossButton">\n'[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    for (const buttonClass of classes) {[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const myFullClass = await store.getResourceAsync(buttonClass);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const shortname = myFullClass.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/shortname");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        let color = myFullClass.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/color");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const parentUrl = myFullClass.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/parent").toString();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const parentRes = await store.getResourceAsync(parentUrl);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const parent = parentRes.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/name");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const description = myFullClass.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/description");[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (!color) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            color = getRandomColor();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        color = hexToRgba(color, 0.5);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const complementaryColor = getComplementaryColor(color);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        let myButtonConcept = buttonClass.toString();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const htmlButton = (shortname, color, complementaryColor, description, myButtonConcept) => `[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <button [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                style="background-color: ${color}; color: ${complementaryColor}; border: 2px solid ${complementaryColor}; font-weight: bold;" [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                onclick="conceptButtonFunction('${shortname}', '${color}', '${myButtonConcept}')" [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                title="${description}">[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                ${shortname}[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            </button>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        `;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (!buttonGroups[parent]) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            buttonGroups[parent] = [];[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        buttonGroups[parent].push(htmlButton(shortname, color, complementaryColor, description, myButtonConcept).trim());[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let groupedButtons = Object.entries(buttonGroups).map(([parent, buttons]) => `[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        <div class="babyBossButton">[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <button class="collapsible">${parent}</button>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <div class="collapsible-content" style="display: none;">[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                ${buttons.join('\n')}[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    `).join('\n');[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    buttonHTML += groupedButtons + '\n</div>'[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    postMessage({[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        type: 'conceptButtons',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        buttons: buttonHTML[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1masync function handleImageInserter(myVisual, container, selectedText, infoToLookFor) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const inputFor = myVisual.get("https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/property/is-input-for");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    //console.log('handleImageInserter', inputFor)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const individualID = inputFor;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    infoToLookFor.push(inputFor);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let dropdown = `[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        <div class="wiserModal">[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <label for="${inputFor}" class="textInfo">Image Inserter</label>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <div class="pasteArea" id="${individualID}">Paste your image here (Ctrl + V)</div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <label for="${inputFor}-description" class="textInfo">Image Description</label>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <textarea id="${inputFor}-description" class="textareaField" placeholder="Enter image description here..."></textarea>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    `;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Add the dropdown to the container[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    container += dropdown;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // JavaScript code as a string[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const laScript = `[0m
[1m[38;5;1mfunction waitForElement(id, callback) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        for (let mutation of mutations) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (mutation.type === 'childList') {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const element = document.getElementById(id);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    observer.disconnect();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    callback(element);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Check if the element already exists[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const element = document.getElementById(id);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        observer.disconnect();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        callback(element);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1mwaitForElement('${individualID}', (element) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    element.addEventListener('paste', async (event) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Prevent the default paste behavior[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        event.preventDefault();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Get the items from the clipboard[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const items = event.clipboardData.items;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Loop through the clipboard items[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        for (const item of items) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // Check if the item is an image[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (item.type.startsWith('image/')) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Get the image file as a blob[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const blob = item.getAsFile();[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Create a FileReader to read the image file[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const reader = new FileReader();[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Define what happens when the reader loads the file[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                reader.onload = (e) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // The result is a base64 encoded data URL[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const base64Data = e.target.result;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // Set the base64 data URL as a data attribute on the div[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.setAttribute('data-image', base64Data);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.setAttribute('id', "${inputFor}");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // Change the div text to indicate success[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.textContent = 'Image Pasted!';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // Set the background of the div to the pasted image[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.style.backgroundImage = 'url(' + base64Data + ')';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.style.backgroundSize = 'contain';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.style.backgroundRepeat = 'no-repeat';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // Make the text transparent so it doesn't overlap with the image[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    element.style.color = 'transparent';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                };[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Read the image file as a base64 encoded data URL[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                reader.readAsDataURL(blob);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }else{[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                alert('No image in clipboard found');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m});[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1mwaitForElement('${inputFor}-description', (textarea) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    textarea.addEventListener('input', () => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const element = document.getElementById('${individualID}');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            element.setAttribute('data-description', textarea.value);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m`;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        container, laScript[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    };[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1masync function handleDropDown(myVisual, container, selectedText, infoToLookFor) {[0m

[1m[38;5;1m    console.log('handleDropdown', inputFor)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const optionClass = myVisual.get("https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/property/option-class");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let listName = ""[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let myClasses = [][0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (!optionClass) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // then there I am aiming for something bigger[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        let optionParentClass = myVisual.get("https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/property/option-parent-class")[0m

[1m[38;5;1m        let parentClasses = parentRes.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/classes");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        let finalMyClassesContainingDuplicates = [][0m
[1m[38;5;1m        for (const parentClass of parentClasses) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const blogCollection = new CollectionBuilder(store)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                .setProperty(core.properties.isA)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                .setValue(parentClass)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                .setPageSize(100)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                .build();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            let tmpMembers = await blogCollection.getAllMembers(); // string[][0m
[1m[38;5;1m            console.log('may I present? all the members of', parentClass)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            for (const member of tmpMembers) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                console.log('push member', member)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                finalMyClassesContainingDuplicates.push(member)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        myClasses = finalMyClassesContainingDuplicates[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Retrieve the list of all the instances of the option class[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const optionClassResource = await store.getResourceAsync(optionClass);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        listName = optionClassResource.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/shortname");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const blogCollection = new CollectionBuilder(store)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .setProperty(core.properties.isA)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .setValue(optionClass)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .setPageSize(100)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .build();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        myClasses = await blogCollection.getAllMembers(); // string[][0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    infoToLookFor.push(inputFor);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let optionsHTML = '';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let optionValues = [];[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Generate options and store option values[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    for (const key of myClasses) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        //console.log('dropdown heading for key', key)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if(key){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const snResource = await store.getResourceAsync(key);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            let optionValue = snResource.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/shortname");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            let comment = snResource.get("https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/property/wiser-comment");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (comment) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                optionValue += ": " + comment;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            optionValues.push({key, optionValue});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            optionsHTML += `<option class="dropdown" value="${key}">${optionValue}</option>`;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let randomValue = ([1e7] + -1e3 + -4e3 + -8e3 + -1e11).replace(/[018-]/g, c =>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        (c ^ crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(1))[0] & 15 >> c / 4).toString(16)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    ).replace(/-/g, '_');[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let dropdown = `[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        <div class="wiserModal">[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <div class="textInfo">Dropdown</div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <label class="wiserSearchLabel" for="${inputFor}">${listName}</label>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <input class="wiserSearchInput" type="text" id="search-${inputFor.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, '')}" placeholder="Search ${listName}...">[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <select class="dropdown" name="${inputFor}" id="${inputFor}">[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                <option class="dropdown" value="" selected disabled hidden>Select an option</option>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                ${optionsHTML}[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            </select>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    `;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Add the dropdown to the container[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    container += dropdown;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let functionName = "eventFunction_" + randomValue;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // JavaScript code as a string[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const laScript = `[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        function checkElementExistence(elementId, eventType, ${functionName}, intervalTime = 100) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const intervalId = setInterval(function() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const element = document.getElementById(elementId);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    clearInterval(intervalId);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    addEventListenerToElement(element, eventType, ${functionName});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }, intervalTime);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        function addEventListenerToElement(element, eventType, ${functionName}) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            element.addEventListener(eventType, ${functionName});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Define the event function[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const ${functionName} = function() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const searchValue = this.value.toLowerCase();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const dropdown = document.getElementById('${inputFor}');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            dropdown.innerHTML = '';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const filteredOptions = ${JSON.stringify(optionValues)}.filter(option =>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                option.optionValue.toLowerCase().includes(searchValue)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            );[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            for (const option of filteredOptions) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const optionElement = document.createElement('option');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                optionElement.value = option.key;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                optionElement.text = option.optionValue;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                optionElement.classList.add('dropdown');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                dropdown.appendChild(optionElement);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        };[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Call the function with appropriate parameters[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        checkElementExistence('search-${inputFor.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, '')}', 'input', ${functionName});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    `;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        container, laScript[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    };[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1mfunction getLastPartOfURL(url) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const parts = url.split('/');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return parts[parts.length - 1];[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1masync function createModal(url, magic, selectedText = '') {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    console.log('going for concept', url)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const concept = await store.getResourceAsync(url)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const lastPart = getLastPartOfURL(url)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const potentialSubject = store.createSubject(lastPart)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const description = concept.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/description")[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const shortName = concept.get("https://atomicdata.dev/properties/shortname")[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const visuals = concept.get("https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/property/has-visuals")[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let infoToLookFor = [][0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let laFinalScript = "";[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let laScript;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let container = '<div>'[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    container += `[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    <h2 class="title"> ${shortName} </h2>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    <div class="textInfo">${description}</div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                `[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    for (const visualIndex in visuals) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const myVisual = await store.getResourceAsync(visuals[visualIndex])[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // only one class is allowed anyway[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const clazz = myVisual.getClasses()[0];[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // define container[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        switch (clazz) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            case "https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/class/textarea-visual":[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                container = await handleTextArea(myVisual, container, selectedText, infoToLookFor);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            case "https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/class/dropdown-visual":[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                ({container, laScript} = await handleDropDown(myVisual, container, selectedText, infoToLookFor));[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            case "https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/class/checkbox-visual":[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                container = await handleCheckbox(myVisual, container, infoToLookFor);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            case "https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/class/insert-image-visual":[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                ({container, laScript} = await handleImageInserter(myVisual, container, selectedText, infoToLookFor));[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            default:[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if(laScript){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            laFinalScript += laScript;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            laScript = null;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    //close container[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    laScript = laFinalScript[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    container += '</div>'[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const myDiv = container[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    postMessage({[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        type: 'pong',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        magic,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        content: myDiv,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        infoToLookFor,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        potentialSubject,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        laScript[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1masync function handleKnowledgeUpdate(message) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Retrieve elements with the class 'rdfa_content' and their children[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const $ = cheerio.load(message.document);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const rdfasInHTML = $('.rdfa-content')[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const updatedElements = [][0m
[1m[38;5;1m    for (const rdfaElement of rdfasInHTML) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const cheerioElement = $(rdfaElement);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const childrenWithTypeof = cheerioElement.find('[typeof]');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (childrenWithTypeof.length > 0) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // only update the ones with a potential-wiser-id[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const potentialID = $(childrenWithTypeof[0]).attr('data-wiser-potential-subject')[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (potentialID) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const newId = $(childrenWithTypeof[0]).attr('data-wiser-id')[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const className = $(childrenWithTypeof[0]).attr('typeof')[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const newSubject = potentialID[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                //TODO: check for the same WISER-ID[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (await store.checkSubjectTaken(newSubject)) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    console.log("subject already taken, react to it", newSubject)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    //return[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const newResource = new Resource(newSubject);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const reallyNewResource = await store.newResource(newResource)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    if (newId) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        await reallyNewResource.set("https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch/property/wiser-id", newId, store);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        await reallyNewResource.set(core.properties.shortname, newId, store);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    await reallyNewResource.addClasses(store, className.toString());[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    for (const child of childrenWithTypeof[0].children) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        const prop = $(child).attr('property')[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        const val = $(child).attr('data-wiser-content')[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        await reallyNewResource.set(prop, val, store)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const commit = await reallyNewResource.save(store);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // TODO: make a better check, whether the element go really created[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    if (commit) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        updatedElements.push(newSubject)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // here I can give the infos I want to for the PDF save after everything is done[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    postMessage({[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        type: 'updatePDFAfterKGAdd',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        updatedElements[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    })[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1monmessage = async (e) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const message = e.data;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (!message || !message.type) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        console.error("Received message without type:", message);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        postMessage({type: 'error', error: 'Message type is required'});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    switch (message.type) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        case 'getConcepts':[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            await handleRetrieveConcepts();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            break[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        case 'getResource':[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (!message.url) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                postMessage({type: 'getResource', status: 'error', error: 'URL is required'});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            await handleGetResource(message.url);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        case 'addKnowledge':[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (!message.document) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                postMessage({type: 'addKnowledge', status: 'error', error: 'Document is required'});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                return[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            await handleKnowledgeUpdate(message)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        case 'ping':[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (!message.magic || !message.url) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                postMessage({type: 'ping', status: 'error', error: 'magic and url is required'});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const gotRes = await store.checkSubjectTaken(message.url)[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            postMessage({[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                type: 'pong',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                magic: message.magic,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                content: gotRes[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        case 'createModal':[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (!message.url || !message.magic) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                postMessage({type: 'createModal', status: 'error', error: 'I need to have a url and a magic word'})[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (message.selectedText) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                await createModal(message.url, message.magic, message.selectedText)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                await createModal(message.url, message.magic)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        default:[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            console.error("Unknown message type:", message.type);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            postMessage({type: 'error', error: 'Unknown message type'});[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m};[0m

[1m[38;5;1masync function init() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const serverURL = "https://wiser-sp4.interactions.ics.unisg.ch";[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    await store.setServerUrl(serverURL);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Fetch key and URL from the endpoint[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const response = await fetch('/v1/api/get_my_agent');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (!response.ok) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        throw new Error(`Failed to fetch agent details: ${response.statusText}`);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const agentData = await response.json();[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    myAgent = new Agent([0m
[1m[38;5;1m        agentData.key,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        agentData.url[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    );[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    await store.setAgent(myAgent);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    console.log("Atomic Worker: Store initialized successfully");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1masync function handleGetResource(url) {[0m

[1m[38;5;1mfunction createHTMLStringFromObject(obj) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return '';[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Start the element with the tagName[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let htmlString = `<${obj.tagName.toLowerCase()}`;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let wiser_content = null[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Add the attributes[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (obj.attributes) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        for (let attr in obj.attributes) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            //ignore the first id, because this was generated by the tool and might be the same again[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if(attr !== "id"){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                htmlString += ` ${attr}="${obj.attributes[attr]}"`;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if(attr === "data-wiser-content"){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                wiser_content = obj.attributes[attr][0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            //transform the ids I want to actual IDs[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if(attr === "data-wiser-id"){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                htmlString += ` id="${obj.attributes[attr]}"`[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Close the opening tag[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    htmlString += '>';[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Add the content if it exists[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (obj.content) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        htmlString += obj.content;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    else if(wiser_content){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        htmlString += wiser_content[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Process children recursively[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (obj.children && Array.isArray(obj.children)) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        obj.children.forEach(childObj => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            htmlString += createHTMLStringFromObject(childObj);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Add the closing tag[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    htmlString += `</${obj.tagName.toLowerCase()}>`;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return htmlString;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m

[1m[38;5;1mfunction wiserSerializeHTMLElement(element, helper) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  const serializedElements = [];[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m  // Get the scale factor from the element with the id "viewer"[0m

[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m  // Serialize any element with its children[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  function serializeElementWithChildren(element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const elementObj = {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      tagName: element.tagName,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      attributes: {},[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      content: element.ariaLabel, // capture the inner HTML of the element[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      children: [],[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      scaleFactor, // add the scale factor[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    };[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Serialize attributes[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    Array.from(element.attributes).forEach(attr => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      elementObj.attributes[attr.name] = attr.value;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Serialize children[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    Array.from(element.children).forEach(child => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      elementObj.children.push(serializeElementWithChildren(child));[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return elementObj;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m  function extractBaseInfo(expression) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const regex = /(\d+\.?\d*)px/;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const matches = expression.match(regex);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return matches ? parseFloat(matches[1]) : null;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m  // Find the closest parent with the class "page" and return its height[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  function analyzePageOfMark(element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let parent = element.parentElement;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    while (parent && !parent.classList.contains("page")) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      parent = parent.parentElement;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const myHeight = parent.style.getPropertyValue("height");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const myWidth = parent.style.getPropertyValue("width");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const pageNumber = parseInt(parent.dataset.pageNumber);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (pageNumber === undefined) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      console.error("Page number not found");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const baseHeight = extractBaseInfo(myHeight);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const baseWidth = extractBaseInfo(myWidth);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const returner = {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      baseHeight,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      baseWidth,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      pageNumber,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    };[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    return returner;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  }[0m

[1m[38;5;1m  // Find all mark elements and serialize their grandparent if it's 'div'[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  function findAndSerializeMarks(element) {[0m

[1m[38;5;1m      // Check if the parent is 'div'[0m

[1m[38;5;1m        const exactLocation = calculateElementPositionAndSize(parentSerialized);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        parentSerialized.exactLocation = exactLocation;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        serializedElements.push(parentSerialized);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      // Recurse through child elements[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      Array.from(element.children).forEach(findAndSerializeMarks);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m  function calculateElementPositionAndSize(element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Extract style attributes[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const actualHeight = element.actualHeight;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const actualWidth = element.actualWidth;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const style = element.attributes.style;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const styles = style.split(";").reduce((acc, current) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      const [key, value] = current.split(":").map(item => item.trim());[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      if (key && value) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        acc[key] = value;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      return acc;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }, {});[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Calculate position and size[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const left = (parseFloat(styles.left) / 100) * actualWidth;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const top = (parseFloat(styles.top) / 100) * actualHeight;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const width = (parseFloat(styles.width) / 100) * actualWidth;[0m

[1m[38;5;1mfunction getLastPartOfUrl(url) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Split the URL by the '/' character[0m

[1m[38;5;1m                    mode: 0,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        },[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        /**[0m
[1m[38;5;1m         * Handles the close operation.[0m
[1m[38;5;1m         */[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        onClose() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            uiManager._eventBus.dispatch("switchannotationeditormode",[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    source: this,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    mode: 0,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            myHide()[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    };[0m
}

[1m[38;5;1mexport {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    EditorToolbar,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    HighlightToolbar[0m
[1m[38;5;1m};[0m

[38;5;11mdeleted: [7mweb/WiserEventBus.js[0m
[38;5;11m-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------[0m
[1m[38;5;13m@ web/WiserEventBus.js:1 @[1m[0m
[1m[38;5;1mconst WiserEventBus = {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    events: {},[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    on(event, listener) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (!this.events[event]) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            this.events[event] = [];[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.events[event].push(listener);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    },[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    off(event, listenerToRemove) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (!this.events[event]) return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.events[event] = this.events[event].filter(listener => listener !== listenerToRemove);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    },[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    emit(event, data) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (!this.events[event]) return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.events[event].forEach(listener => listener(data));[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    },[0m
[1m[38;5;1m};[0m
[1m[38;5;1mexport default WiserEventBus;[0m

[1m[38;5;1m        issues.[0m

[1m[38;5;1m    let choice = false[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    let finalFilename = filename[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // if saving-done is true, we don't have to ask, we go directly to update[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if(!savingDone){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      console.log("this is a normal save")[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      const finalFilename = prompt("Please enter the filename:", filename);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      // Ask user whether they want to save it to the server or download the PDF[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      choice = confirm("Do you want to save it to the server? Click 'OK' to save to server, 'Cancel' to download the PDF.");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (choice || savingDone) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      console.log("saving it with savingDone", savingDone)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      // User chose to save it to the server[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      saveToServer(new Blob([data], { type: "application/pdf" }), finalFilename, savingDone);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      // allow the saving of knowledge now[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      const subTitleComponent = document.getElementById("myPDFTitle")[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      if(subTitleComponent){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          subTitleComponent.textContent = subTitleComponent.textContent.replace("*","")[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      if(saveKGButton){[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          // remove the saving done for sure[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          saveKGButton.removeAttribute("saving-done")[0m
[1m[38;5;2m    let blobUrl;[0m
[1m[38;5;2m    if (data) {[0m
[1m[38;5;2m      blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL([0m
[1m[38;5;2m        new Blob([data], { type: "application/pdf" })[0m
[1m[38;5;2m      );[0m
[1m[38;5;2m    } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;2m      if (!createValidAbsoluteUrl(url, "http://example.com")) {[0m
[1m[38;5;2m        console.error(`download - not a valid URL: ${url}`);[0m
[1m[38;5;2m        return;[0m
      }
[1m[38;5;1m    }else{[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      let blobUrl;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      if (data) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL([0m
[1m[38;5;1m              new Blob([data], { type: "application/pdf" })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          );[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          if (!createValidAbsoluteUrl(url, "http://example.com")) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              console.error(`download - not a valid URL: ${url}`);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          blobUrl = url + "#pdfjs.action=download";[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      download(blobUrl, filename);[0m
[1m[38;5;2m      blobUrl = url + "#pdfjs.action=download";[0m
    }
[1m[38;5;2m    download(blobUrl, filename);[0m
  }
}

[1m[38;5;1m<script>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    function checkViewer() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Use a delay to allow HTMX to load content, or adjust according to how HTMX operates[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const intervalId = setInterval(() => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const pdfTitle = document.getElementById("myPDFTitle")[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const viewerExists = pdfTitle.textContent.length > 4[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const elements = document.getElementsByClassName("pdf_utils");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            for (let elementsKey in elements) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (elements[elementsKey].style) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    elements[elementsKey].style.display = viewerExists ? 'block' : 'none'[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const openElement = document.getElementById("pdf_open");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (!viewerExists) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                openElement.style.display = 'block'[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (viewerExists) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                clearInterval(intervalId)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }, 1000); // Adjust timeout as needed based on testing[0m

[1m[38;5;1m    document.getElementById("pdfInput").addEventListener('change', (event) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const file = event.target.files[0];[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (file && file.type === "application/pdf") {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const formData = new FormData();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const originalFileName = file.name;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const slugifiedFileName = sluggify(originalFileName);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            formData.append('file', file, slugifiedFileName);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            fetch('/v1/api/upload', {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                method: 'POST',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                body: formData[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                .then(response => response.text())[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                .then(data => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    if (data) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        console.log("data", data)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        const filenameWithoutExtension = slugifiedFileName.replace('.pdf', '');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        window.location.href = `/v1/api/pdf/${filenameWithoutExtension}`;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        alert('Failed to upload PDF');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                .catch(error => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    console.error('Error:', error);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    alert('An error occurred while uploading the PDF');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            alert('Please select a PDF file.');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    function sluggify(filename) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const extension = filename.split('.').pop();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const name = filename.substring(0, filename.lastIndexOf('.'));[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const slugifiedName = name[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .toString()[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .toLowerCase()[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .replace(/\s+/g, '-')           // Replace spaces with -[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .replace(/[^\w\-]+/g, '')       // Remove all non-word chars[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .replace(/\-\-+/g, '-')         // Replace multiple - with single -[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .replace(/^-+/, '')             // Trim - from start of text[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .replace(/-+$/, '');            // Trim - from end of text[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        return `${slugifiedName}.${extension}`;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    document.getElementById("syncPDF").addEventListener('click', (event) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Get the current window location[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const currentLocation = window.location.href;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Extract the last part of the URL after the last slash[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const pdfUrl = currentLocation.substring(currentLocation.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Construct the API URL[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const apiUrl = `/v1/api/update/${pdfUrl}`;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Make a GET request to the constructed API URL[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        fetch(apiUrl, {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            method: 'GET'[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .then(response => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (!response.ok) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    throw new Error('Network response was not ok');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                return response.text();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .then(data => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                alert("Syncing was successful", data)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            .catch(error => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                console.error('There has been a problem with your fetch operation:', error);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m

[1m[38;5;1m            alert(prefix + " element(s) were updated");[0m

[1m[38;5;1m            window.wiserEventBus.off('knowledgeConfirmation', knowledgeConfirmationListener);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        };[0m

[1m[38;5;1m    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const buttonContainer = document.querySelector('#right-sidebar .button-container');[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        buttonContainer.addEventListener('click', function (event) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (event.target.tagName === 'BUTTON') {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Check if the button does not have the 'collapsible' class[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (!event.target.classList.contains('collapsible')) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // Remove the highlighted class from all buttons[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const buttons = buttonContainer.querySelectorAll('button');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    buttons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('highlightedConceptButton'));[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    // Add the highlighted class to the clicked button[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    event.target.classList.add('highlightedConceptButton');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    });[0m

[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    function attachCollapsibleEventListeners() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const collapsibleElements = document.querySelectorAll('.collapsible');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (collapsibleElements.length > 0) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            collapsibleElements.forEach(button => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (!button.hasAttribute('data-listener-attached')) { // Check if listener is already attached[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    button.addEventListener('click', () => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        const content = button.nextElementSibling;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        content.style.display = content.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    button.setAttribute('data-listener-attached', 'true'); // Mark this element as having a listener[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            return true; // Indicate that collapsible elements were found[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        return false; // Indicate that no collapsible elements were found[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    // Periodically check for new collapsible elements every second[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    const intervalId = setInterval(() => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const found = attachCollapsibleEventListeners();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        if (found) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop the interval if collapsible elements are found[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }, 1000);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m</script>[0m

[1m[38;5;1m            const escape = {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                '&': '&amp;',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                '<': '&lt;',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                '>': '&gt;',[0m

[1m[38;5;1m                "'": '&#039;'[0m

[7m[7m [0m

[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m      async function downloadRDF() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const mainContent = document.getElementById("embeddedIframe");[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        let triples = [];[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // access iframe window object[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const iframe = document.getElementById("embeddedIframe");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const iframeWindow = iframe.contentWindow;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const myParser = iframeWindow.myParser;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        myParser[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          .on("data", data => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if (data.predicate.value.includes("xhtml")) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              return;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            if ([0m
[1m[38;5;1m              data.subject.termType === "NamedNode" &&[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              data.predicate.termType === "NamedNode" &&[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              data.object.termType === "NamedNode"[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            ) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              triples.push([0m
[1m[38;5;1m                `<${data.subject.value}> <${data.predicate.value}> <${data.object.value}> .`[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              );[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            } else {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              triples.push([0m
[1m[38;5;1m                `<${data.subject.value}> <${data.predicate.value}> "${data.object.value}" .`[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              );[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          .on("error", console.error)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          .on("end", () => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // Create a Blob from the triples array[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const turtleData = triples.join("\n");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const blob = new Blob([turtleData], { type: "text/turtle" });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // Create a download link and trigger the download[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            const a = document.createElement("a");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            a.href = url;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            a.download = "knowledge.ttl";[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            document.body.appendChild(a);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            a.click();[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // Cleanup: revoke the blob URL and remove the link[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            document.body.removeChild(a);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const iframeDocument = iframe.contentDocument;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        console.log("mainContent", iframeDocument);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const content = iframeDocument.documentElement.innerHTML;[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Use the content as needed, for example, logging it or passing it to a function[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        console.log("Document innerHTML:", content);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        await myParser.write(content);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        await myParser.end();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    </script>[0m

[1m[38;5;1m                            >Creation Date: 2024-04-26</span[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                          >[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                      </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                  </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            <!-- Tailwind 'hidden' class for initial state -->[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          </div>[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m          <script>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              const retrieveContentBtn =[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                document.getElementById("retrieveContentBtn");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              const kgShow = document.getElementById("kgShow");[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m              // Function to retrieve content[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              function retrieveContent() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Toggle display using Tailwind CSS classes[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                kgShow.innerHTML = "";[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const element = document.getElementById("documentID");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                  const documentID = element.getAttribute("data-content");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                  if (documentID && documentID.length > 0) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const htmxButton = document.createElement("button");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    htmxButton.setAttribute([0m
[1m[38;5;1m                      "hx-get",[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                      `/pdf/annotations/${documentID}`[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    );[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    htmxButton.setAttribute("hx-target", "#kgShow");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    htmxButton.setAttribute("hx-swap", "innerHTML");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    htmxButton.setAttribute("hidden", "true");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    kgShow.appendChild(htmxButton);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    htmx.process(htmxButton);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    htmxButton.click();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    clearInterval(checkDocumentIDInterval); // Stop checking once a valid documentID is found[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                  }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m              // Function to toggle visibility[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              function toggleVisibility() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                kgShow.classList.toggle("hidden");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                retrieveContent();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m              // Toggle content display on button click[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              retrieveContentBtn.addEventListener("click", toggleVisibility);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m              // Check for a valid documentID every 100 ms[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              const checkDocumentIDInterval = setInterval(function () {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const element = document.getElementById("documentID");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                if (element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                  const documentID = element.getAttribute("data-content");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                  if (documentID && documentID.length > 0) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    retrieveContent(); // Call retrieveContent if a valid documentID is found[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                  }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m              }, 100);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m              retrieveContent();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          </script>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      </aside>[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m      <script>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        function changeHighlightColor(color, concept, element) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          const sidebar = document.getElementById("sidebar");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          sidebar.setAttribute("data-highlight-color", color);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          sidebar.setAttribute("data-highlight-concept", concept);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m          //TODO: for the modal, create the corresponding rdfa_data[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          //TODO: add login with WISER and AtomicData somehow[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          // Remove active classes from all buttons[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          document.querySelectorAll(".concept-btn").forEach(btn => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            btn.classList.remove("bg-gray-200", "text-green-500");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            btn.classList.add("bg-green-500", "text-white");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m          // Add active class to the clicked button[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          element.classList.add("bg-gray-200", "text-green-500"); // Indicate active state[0m
[1m[38;5;1m          element.classList.remove("bg-green-500", "text-white");[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m      </script>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    </div>[0m
[1m[38;5;1m  </body>[0m

function webViewerLoad() {
[1m[38;5;1m    const config = getViewerConfiguration();[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    if (typeof PDFJSDev !== "undefined" && PDFJSDev.test("GENERIC")) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // Give custom implementations of the default viewer a simpler way to[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // set various `AppOptions`, by dispatching an event once all viewer[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // files are loaded but *before* the viewer initialization has run.[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const event = new CustomEvent("webviewerloaded", {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            bubbles: true,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            cancelable: true,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            detail: {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                source: window,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            },[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        try {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // Attempt to dispatch the event at the embedding `document`,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // in order to support cases where the viewer is embedded in[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // a *dynamically* created <iframe> element.[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            parent.document.dispatchEvent(event);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        } catch (ex) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // The viewer could be in e.g. a cross-origin <iframe> element,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            // fallback to dispatching the event at the current `document`.[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            console.error(`webviewerloaded: ${ex}`);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            document.dispatchEvent(event);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        }[0m
[1m[38;5;2m  const config = getViewerConfiguration();[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;2m  if (typeof PDFJSDev !== "undefined" && PDFJSDev.test("GENERIC")) {[0m
[1m[38;5;2m    // Give custom implementations of the default viewer a simpler way to[0m
[1m[38;5;2m    // set various `AppOptions`, by dispatching an event once all viewer[0m

[1m[38;5;2m    });[0m
[1m[38;5;2m    try {[0m

[1m[38;5;2m      // a *dynamically* created <iframe> element.[0m
[1m[38;5;2m      parent.document.dispatchEvent(event);[0m
[1m[38;5;2m    } catch (ex) {[0m

[1m[38;5;2m      // fallback to dispatching the event at the current `document`.[0m

[1m[38;5;1m    PDFViewerApplication.run(config);[0m

// Block the "load" event until all pages are loaded, to ensure that printing

[1m[38;5;1mclass Modal {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    constructor() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.modalRoot = document.getElementById('modal-root');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.initStore().then((success) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            WiserEventBus.on('showModal', this.showModal.bind(this));[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            WiserEventBus.on('downloadKnowledge', () => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Extract the HTML content as a string[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                const documentHTML = document.documentElement.outerHTML;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                window.myAtomicWorker.postMessage({[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    type: 'addKnowledge',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    document: documentHTML[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m            window.wiserEventBus = WiserEventBus[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        })[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    async initStore() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        window.myAtomicWorker.onmessage = async (e) => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            switch (e.data.type) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                case "pong":[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const magicWord = e.data.magic;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const content = e.data.content;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const infoToLookFor = e.data.infoToLookFor;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const potentialSubject = e.data.potentialSubject;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    const laScript = e.data.laScript;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    WiserEventBus.emit(magicWord, {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        content,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        infoToLookFor,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        potentialSubject,[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                        laScript[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    });[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                case "conceptButtons":[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    await handleConceptButtons(e.data);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                // Add more cases here as needed[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                case 'updatePDFAfterKGAdd':[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    await handleUpdatePDFAfterKGAdd(e.data, document)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                case 'ping':[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    //ignore[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    break;[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                default:[0m
[1m[38;5;1m                    console.log("not yet implemented type", e)[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        };[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        // now init the buttons[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        window.myAtomicWorker.postMessage({[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            type: 'getConcepts',[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            user: 'potentialUser'[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        window.myAtomicWorker = myAtomicWorker[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    /**[0m
[1m[38;5;1m     * Function that accepts any object adhering to the IModal interface.[0m
[1m[38;5;1m     * @param {IModal} modal - An object that implements the IModal interface.[0m
[1m[38;5;1m     */[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    async showModal(modal) {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.clearModal();[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const modalOverlay = document.createElement('div');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        modalOverlay.className = 'modal-overlay';[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const modalContent = document.createElement('div');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        modalContent.className = 'modal-content';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        modalOverlay.appendChild(modalContent);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const content = document.createElement('div');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        content.innerHTML = await modal.render(window.myAtomicWorker);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        modalContent.appendChild(content);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const footer = document.createElement('div');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        footer.className = 'modal-footer';[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const saveButton = document.createElement('button');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        saveButton.textContent = 'Save';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        saveButton.addEventListener('click', async () => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            await modal.onSave(window.myAtomicWorker);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            this.clearModal();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        const closeButton = document.createElement('button');[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        closeButton.textContent = 'Close';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        closeButton.addEventListener('click', async () => {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            await modal.onClose();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m            this.clearModal();[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        });[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        footer.appendChild(saveButton);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        footer.appendChild(closeButton);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        modalContent.appendChild(footer);[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.modalRoot.appendChild(modalOverlay);[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[7m[7m [0m
[1m[38;5;1m    clearModal() {[0m
[1m[38;5;1m        this.modalRoot.innerHTML = '';[0m
[1m[38;5;1m    }[0m
[1m[38;5;1m}[0m
